## 公式

### FORM-001

- model_id: `MOD-001`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `candidate = None if no trigger match or normalized statement length < 8. Else classify_chunk uses priority temporary_or_sensitive unless temp_is_rule, deprecated_info, security_boundary, decision, answering_rule, workflow, project_context, preference, else fact. Importance maps security_boundary/decision/answering_rule to 高, workflow/project_context/preference/deprecated_info to 中, else 低. Validity maps temporary_or_sensitive to 临时, project_context to 项目结束前, workflow/preference to 半年, else 长期. Confidence is high if trigger_count >= 3 or importance == 高, medium if trigger_count >= 1, else low. assign_memory_tier returns 临时 for sensitive/secret or 临时 validity, 核心画像 for preference/answering_rule/core profile regex, 一般 for decision/project_context/workflow/security_boundary or long/project/half-year validity, else 临时. merge key is category + normalized statement; evidence is capped at 10; medium confidence promotes to high after evidence_count >= 3.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-002

- model_id: `MOD-002`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `redact_text replaces SECRET_PATTERNS and PII_PATTERNS findings before candidate persistence. In make_candidate, secret_types excluding email/phone produce secret_ref = stable_id('secretref', source + conversation_id + normalized redacted text + secret types) and sensitivity secret. Non-secret defaults to private. temporary_or_sensitive becomes sensitive unless already secret and statement is replaced with a redacted_source_hash prefix of sha256(redacted)[:16]. OpenAI-export decision/project/workflow/deprecated candidates without meta_context become sensitive. security_boundary becomes sensitive unless secret. secret_ref candidates receive credential_policy plaintext_in_git=false, agent_access authorized_local_secret_resolver_only, requires_user_authorization=true, local_resolver_required=true, trading boundary fail closed.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-003

- model_id: `MOD-003`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `normalized_memory_tier first demotes code/config noise to 临时, then applies aliases 重要中长期->一般 and 一般短期->临时, else uses stored tier if valid, else assign_memory_tier. retrieval_weight maps 核心画像 to high, 一般 to medium, all other tiers to low. build_active_memory_rows copies each candidate, normalizes tier, applies curation override fields, sets status active, review_status active_auto_promoted_from_full_flow, activation_mode user_authorized_full_flow, and derives use_when/do_not_use_for from tier and secret status.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-004

- model_id: `MOD-004`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `build_sqlite_index creates memory table and inserts active/candidate records except rows where sensitivity == secret. query_index builds WHERE sensitivity != secret plus AND over query terms where each term matches statement OR category OR source via LIKE. SQL order is date DESC, importance ASC and LIMIT limit*5. Post-filter keeps rows with SENSITIVITY_RANK <= rank(sensitivity_max) until limit. fetch_index returns not_found when absent, redacted_secret when record sensitivity is secret, otherwise the redacted record JSON.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-005

- model_id: `MOD-005`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `tier_score = TIER_WEIGHT.get(normalize_tier(memory_tier), 0.25); importance_score = IMPORTANCE_WEIGHT.get(importance, 0.35); confidence_score = CONFIDENCE_WEIGHT.get(confidence, 0.6); weight_score = round(tier_score*0.5 + importance_score*0.3 + confidence_score*0.2, 4). Memory node visual size = round(4 + weight_score*8, 3); brightness = confidence score rounded to 3; orbit_radius = round(30 + (1 - weight_score)*76, 3); theme/tier edges use round(weight_score, 4).`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-006

- model_id: `MOD-006`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `recency_days = today - date when date exists. sensitivity_penalty = 0.35 for sensitive or secret else 0.1. staleness_status = stale_short_term when validity == 临时 and recency_days > 30; needs_review when recency_days > 180; current otherwise when date exists; missing-date branch when date is absent. decision_impact = 1 for category decision else 0. leverage_score = round(max(0.0, memory_weight(row) + decision_impact*0.15 - sensitivity_penalty), 4). Recommended action maps 核心画像 to keep_high_weight, 一般 to review_for_project_linkage, stale or needs_review to keep_low_weight_or_refresh, else keep_as_context.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-007

- model_id: `MOD-007`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `activity_score = conversation_count*5 + message_count + memory_count*3 + candidate_count + decision_count*4 + tool_call_count*2 + error_event_count + abort_count*2. activity_level = 0 if score <= 0 or max_score <= 0 else ceil(score/max_score*5) bounded 1..5. Quantile p = sorted_scores[min(n-1, max(0, ceil(p*n)-1))]. Daily range is filled from min to max date and then aggregated to week/month/year.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-008

- model_id: `MOD-008`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `For each Codex session, topic_labels are topic rules with matched counts; signal_labels are signal rules with matched counts. activity_score = message_count + user_message_count*2 + tool_call_count*3 + len(topic_labels)*4 + error_event_count*2. Daily buckets sum session activity_score and derive activity_level = 0 if score <= 0 or max_score <= 0 else max(1, min(5, ceil(score*5/max_score))). Session output stores redacted thread/cwd/model metadata, topic labels, preference signals, top tool counts, and backup_policy redacted_summary_only_no_raw_transcript_no_plaintext_secret.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-009

- model_id: `MOD-009`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `load_data_source_registry returns {} unless schema_version == memory_atlas_data_source_registry.v1 and sources is a list. registry_source_map keeps sources with non-empty id. Acceptance requires sources memory_atlas and codex active; wechat, xiaohongshu, douyin planned; canonical required fields include source_id, record_id, occurred_at, record_type, summary, sensitivity, dedupe_key; homepage data_sources exactly all, memory_atlas, codex with labels 总数据源, ChatGPT, Codex; planned sources must remain registry-only and ingestion_status planned_no_real_data. Static summaries redact private/sensitive/source details before public snapshot.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-010

- model_id: `MOD-010`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `saveProposal requires editable and non-empty draft text. proposal_id = atlas_<compactTimestamp(now)>_<stableHash(node.id:text:nodeProposalCount+1)>; status = draft_pending_agent_apply; revision = latest.revision + 1 or 1; parent_proposal_id = latest proposal id or null; rollback_unit = policy.rollback_unit or per_memory_version; safety direct_frontend_mutation_of_active_memory=false, requires_conflict_check=true, requires_agent_or_human_apply=true, forbidden_payload from policy or plaintext secrets/raw conversation text/record hashes/local absolute paths. createRollbackProposal uses latest and previous/target, action rollback_to_version, revision latest+1, parent latest, supersedes latest, rollback_to_proposal_id target, and rollback_to_revision target revision.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-011

- model_id: `MOD-011`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `build_export_payload loads agent_context_pack plus three_layer_context and resource_routes. It copies layer metadata, sync_required_targets, run_log_categories, startup/chatgpt/codex/project/taste routes, profile, memory, preferences, meta_data, behavior, data_sources, and safety flags. render_chatgpt writes Core Profile, Preferences And Taste, History And Patterns, Project And Decision Context, Future Agent Sync Rules, and Meta Rules. render_codex writes Startup Read Order, Codex Route, Required Sync Targets, Four Run Log Categories, and Agent Rules. route_resources selects exactly one route by intent or fails with valid_intents. evaluate checks required files, required export sections, sync targets, run log categories, and forbidden plaintext patterns. sync_codex_memory_data --build-atlas now rebuilds agent context and personalization exports after Codex-derived data refresh.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-OAIDB-FORMULA-REGISTRY, EVID-SEMANTIC-OAIDB-MANIFEST`

### FORM-MACDATA-PROM2-001

- model_id: `MOD-MACDATA-PROM2-001`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `preflight passes only on macOS when model contains MacBook Pro, chip contains owner-confirmed M2 Max, memory >= 32GB, and owner_confirmations.confirmed_device_key == proM2. Full run writes metrics/report, scans for credential patterns, pushes raw archive to macdata-proM2, verifies remote hash, then cleans macdata retention and owner-confirmed development caches. If push or remote verification fails, cleanup is not executed.`
- evidence_refs: `EVID-MACDATA-PROM2-CONFIG, EVID-MACDATA-PROM2-OWNER-CONFIRMATION`
